**Full child list reconstructed:**
1. John Grice — b. ~1877, West Bromwich (enumerated in all three census years; found with wife Bertha in Birmingham 1901)
2. Lydia Grice — baptized 8 August 1878, West Bromwich (ADDITIONAL CHILD — the answer to q_001)
3. Hannah Grace Grice — baptized ~1880, West Bromwich; died ~1883 West Bromwich (confirmed absent from 1891 census; death index entry ark:/61903/1:1:2JD1-Q7B)

5. William Grice — b. ~1885 West Bromwich (in John's 1901 household)
6. James Grice — baptized 27 October 1886, West Bromwich (in John's 1901 household)

<summary>
The research confirms that **Lydia Grice** (baptized **8 August 1878** in **West Bromwich, Staffordshire, England**) is the one additional child of Hannah Earnest and Edwin Grice beyond the five children named in the project objective (John, Hannah Grace, Edwin, William, and James).

Lydia is documented in three independent sources: her baptism record in the Staffordshire Church Records (father: Edwin Grice, mother: Hannah), the 1881 England census showing her in the Grice household, and the 1891 England census where she continues to appear with her siblings. No further unidentified children were found after searching Staffordshire church baptism records, three census years (1881, 1891, 1901), the England and Wales Birth Registration Index, the Death Registration Index, and the England Births and Christenings collection.

The complete child list for Hannah Earnest and Edwin Grice is: John (~1877), **Lydia (1878)**, Hannah Grace (~1880, died ~1883), Edwin Jr. (~1883), William (~1885), and James (1886). Hannah Earnest herself died in 1888 in West Bromwich, which accounts for no children born after James. Two other Grice children appear in the West Bromwich death index (Sarah d.1877, Ann Maria d.1879) but could not be confirmed as belonging to this family due to absence of matching baptism records.

All plan items have been executed. The research workflow has several GPS steps remaining (record extraction, person-evidence linking, conflict resolution, exhaustiveness evaluation, proof conclusion, and mandatory mentor review) before the project can be formally marked complete, but the substantive research question is answered.
</summary>
